Presents:\nThe Underachievers - Forevermore Express Tour with Pouya & The Buffet Boys + Kirk Knight + Bodega Bamz\n$20 ADV // 8pm // All Ages\n\n\nEast Coast hip-hop duo the Underachievers formed in the Flatbush neighborhood of Brooklyn in 2011, comprised of rappers AK and Issa Gold. AK had originally been using the stage name The Underachiever and applied the moniker to the duo when they began, representing their fondness for smoking weed, experimenting with psychedelic drugs, and other interests which could be seen as symptoms of underachieving by mainstream society. Their curiosity for psychedelics bled through into a somewhat trippy sound that combined frantic rhyme styles with heavy, experimental production. A video for one of the duos early tracks caught the attention of critically acclaimed producer Flying Lotus, who signed the group to his label Brainfeeder Records in 2012 and released two of their mixtapes the next year.
